# <a name="office-client-application-and-platform-availability-for-office-add-ins"></a><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-103">Доступность клиентских приложений и платформ Office для надстроек Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-103">Office client application and platform availability for Office Add-ins</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-104">Работа надстройки Office может зависеть от приложения Office, набора требований, элемента или версии API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-104">To work as expected, your Office Add-in might depend on a specific Office application, a requirement set, an API member, or a version of the API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-105">В таблицах ниже представлены сведения о доступных платформах, точках расширения, наборах обязательных элементов API и общих API, которые в настоящее время поддерживаются для всех приложений Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-105">The following tables contain the available platforms, extension points, API requirement sets, and Common APIs that are currently supported for each Office application.</span></span>

<br>

|<a href="#excel"><img src="../images/index/logo-excel.svg" alt="Excel" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-106"><span>Excel</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-106"><span>Excel</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#onenote"><img src="../images/index/logo-onenote.svg" alt="OneNote" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-107"><span>OneNote</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-107"><span>OneNote</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#outlook"><img src="../images/index/logo-outlook.svg" alt="Outlook" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-108"><span>Outlook</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-108"><span>Outlook</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#powerpoint"><img src="../images/index/logo-powerpoint.svg" alt="PowerPoint" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-109"><span>PowerPoint</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-109"><span>PowerPoint</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#project"><img src="../images/index/logo-project-server.svg" alt="Project" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-110"><span>Project</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-110"><span>Project</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#word"><img src="../images/index/logo-word.svg" alt="Word" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-111"><span>Word</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-111"><span>Word</span></a></span></span>|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-112">Исходный выпуск Office 2016, установленный с помощью MSI, содержит только набор обязательных элементов ExcelApi 1.1, WordApi 1.1 и наборы обязательных элементов общего API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-112">The initial Office 2016 release installed via MSI only contains the ExcelApi 1.1, WordApi 1.1, and Common API requirement sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-113">Дополнительные сведения о журналах обновлений различных версий Office см. в разделе [См. также](#see-also).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-113">For more information about the update history of the various Office versions, check out the [See also](#see-also) section.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-functions-excel-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-358">Пользовательские функции (только Excel)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-358">Custom Functions (Excel only)</span></span>

<table style="width:80%">
  <tr>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-559"><sup>1</sup>Чтобы потребовать набор API удостоверений 1.3 в коде надстройки, проверьте, поддерживается ли он вызовом `isSetSupported('IdentityAPI', '1.3')`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-559"><sup>1</sup> To require Identity API set 1.3 in your add-in code, check if it's supported by calling `isSetSupported('IdentityAPI', '1.3')`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-560">Объявление в манифесте надстройки не поддерживается.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-560">Declaring it in your add-in's manifest isn't supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-561">Также можно определить, поддерживается ли API, проверив, не `undefined` ли он.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-561">You can also determine if the API is supported by checking that it's not `undefined`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-562">Подробнее см. в статье [Использование API из наборов требования более поздних версий](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#using-apis-from-later-requirement-sets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-562">For further details, see [Using APIs from later requirement sets](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#using-apis-from-later-requirement-sets).</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-563"><sup>2</sup> Добавлены обновления после выпуска.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-563"><sup>2</sup> Added with post-release updates.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-564"><sup>3</sup> Поддержка нового пользовательского интерфейса Mac (предварительной версии) доступна в Outlook с версии 16.38.506.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-564"><sup>3</sup> Support for the new Mac UI (preview) is available from Outlook version 16.38.506.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-565">Дополнительные сведения см. в разделе [Поддержка надстроек в Outlook в новом интерфейсе Mac](../outlook/compare-outlook-add-in-support-in-outlook-for-mac.md#add-in-support-in-outlook-on-new-mac-ui-preview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-565">For more information, see the [Add-in support in Outlook on new Mac UI](../outlook/compare-outlook-add-in-support-in-outlook-for-mac.md#add-in-support-in-outlook-on-new-mac-ui-preview) section.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-566">Поддержка клиентами набора обязательных элементов может ограничиваться поддержкой сервера Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-566">Client support for a requirement set may be restricted by Exchange server support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b6f0f-567">Подробные сведения о диапазоне наборов обязательных элементов, поддерживаемых сервером Exchange и клиентами Outlook, см. в статье [Наборы обязательных элементов API JavaScript для Outlook](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#requirement-sets-supported-by-exchange-servers-and-outlook-clients).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b6f0f-567">See [Outlook JavaScript API requirement sets](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#requirement-sets-supported-by-exchange-servers-and-outlook-clients) for details about the range of requirement sets supported by Exchange server and Outlook clients.</span></span>
